    <p>\\n595:     This retention policy can be set per-topic, so a single cluster can have some topics where retention is enforced by size or time and other topics where retention is enforced by     <p>\n595:     This retention policy can be set per-topic, so a single cluster can have some topics where retention is enforced by size or time and other topics where retention is enforced by No attempt is made to move partitions after the fact or balance based on\n57:  * size or I/O rate.\n58:  *\n59:  * A background thread handles log retention by periodically truncating excess log segments.\n60:  */\n61: @threadsafe\n62: class LogManager(logDirs: Seq[File],\n63:                  initialOfflineDirs: Seq[File],\n64:                  configRepository: ConfigRepository,\n65:                  val initialDefaultConfig: LogConfig,\n66:                  val cleanerConfig: CleanerConfig,\n67:                  recoveryThreadsPerDataDir: Int,\n68:                  val flushCheckMs: Long,\n69:                  val flushRecoveryOffsetCheckpointMs: Long,\n70:                  val flushStartOffsetCheckpointMs: Long,\n71:                  val retentionCheckMs: Long,\n72:                  val maxTransactionTimeoutMs: Int,\n73:                  val producerStateManagerConfig: ProducerStateManagerConfig,\n74:                  val producerIdExpirationCheckIntervalMs: Int,\n75:                  scheduler: Scheduler,\n76:                  brokerTopicStats: BrokerTopicStats,\n77:                  logDirFailureChannel: LogDirFailureChannel,\n78:                  time: Time,\n79:                  remoteStorageSystemEnable: Boolean,\n80:                  val initialTaskDelayMs: Long) extends Logging {\n81: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/kafka--0753c489@31d9200189f81283bf60e929ddc38fd68ac034e2/-/blob/core/src/main/scala/kafka/log/LogManager.scala%3FL1-80"}}}

constraints.\\n\\n## Core Retention Enforcement (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java)\\n\\nThe primary enforcement logic resides in UnifiedLog.java, which is the unified log abstraction in Kafka's storage layer. The key method is `deleteOldSegments()` (lines 1894-1902) which orchestrates three types of deletion:\\n\\n1. **Time-Based Retention**: `deleteRetentionMsBreachedSegments()` (lines 1908-1944) - Deletes segments based on their timestamp. For each segment, it checks if `currentTime - segment.largestTimestamp() > retentionMs`. The method logs the deletion reason using either the largest record timestamp or the last modified time of the segment. It respects the `localRetentionMs` configuration for remote-enabled setups.\\n\\n2. **Size-Based Retention**: `deleteRetentionSizeBreachedSegments()` (lines 1946-1975) - Enforces log size limits by calculating if `logSize > retentionSize`. It iteratively removes segments until the log size falls below the configured retention size. Uses `localRetentionSize()` for remote storage scenarios.
